  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_e7927846-3c32-4078-8cfa-a56ca19d65a2'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();

      initializeSiwa();

<span id="freeTextContainer11925715783297706190">There is peace at last between the warrior Clans, and Firestar is proud of the strength and unity of the cats he leads in ThunderClan.   <span id="freeText11925715783297706190" style="display:none">There is peace at last between the warrior Clans, and Firestar is proud of the strength and unity of the cats he leads in ThunderClan. All four forest Clans are thriving, training new warriors and keeping their boundaries without conflict.<br /><br />But Firestar's dreams are haunted by wailing cats fleeing a terrible disaster. With unexpected help from an old kittypet friend, he discovers a shocking secret: StarClan, the warrior ancestors who guide his paw steps, have lied to him.<br /><br />Firestar is faced with the hardest decision of his life. Can he really turn his back on the forest that has become his home and embark on a perilous quest to discover a dark truth--one that has been buried beyond the memory of living cats? Whatever he finds at the end of his journey, he knows that nothing can ever be the same again.</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/16556005" />
    <a title="Annie/Soul" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/942110-annie-soul"><img alt="Annie/Soul" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1273017962p2/942110.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/16556005?book_show_action=true">Feb 27, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie/Soul" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie/Soul" href="/user/show/942110-annie-soul">Annie/Soul</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/942110-annie-soul?shelf=my-favorite-books">my-favorite-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer16556005&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer16556005" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6785030544327459630">THIS IS ONE OF THE BEST BOOKS OF WARRIOR CATS!!! This book takes place RIGHT in between the first series and the second one. Firestar begins to see cats that aren't from Starclan or any other clan! Eventually he finds out that there had been a fifth clan in the forest. Skyclan. A clan that had been driven out of the forest because the twolegs had started building houses on their territory. Firestar and Sandstorm set out to rebuild Skyclan, even through it seems completely impossible! <br/><br/>I LOVE this</span>
  <span id="freeText6785030544327459630" style="display:none">THIS IS ONE OF THE BEST BOOKS OF WARRIOR CATS!!! This book takes place RIGHT in between the first series and the second one. Firestar begins to see cats that aren't from Starclan or any other clan! Eventually he finds out that there had been a fifth clan in the forest. Skyclan. A clan that had been driven out of the forest because the twolegs had started building houses on their territory. Firestar and Sandstorm set out to rebuild Skyclan, even through it seems completely impossible! <br /><br />I LOVE this book soooo much!!! I had read it over and over again. It's filled with adventure in every page! I also liked the new brand of fun, lovable characters that show up, instead of the usual circle of characters from the Clans that we have gotten so used to. I surprise myself by saying that I liked ALL the characters from SkyClan, Ancient and New. </span>
  <a data-text-id="6785030544327459630" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

But this one felt a little bit too long, and I thought if could have used some more work.<br/><br/>Now, it was still a very good book.   <span id="freeText1120972802558772203" style="display:none">After finishing this book, I had an odd feeling of relief that it was over. Now, normally, I LOVE WARRIORS BOOKS. Believe me. But this one felt a little bit too long, and I thought if could have used some more work.<br /><br />Now, it was still a very good book. I actually enjoyed it alot, but it just didn't gel as well as the other Warriors books. I do know that Erin Hunter, the author of the books, is actually three women who write the books together. Maybe they just didn't have much enthusiasm for this book and had to get it in by a certain date. <br /><br />I would give it a 3.5 or 4, because they have a wonderful plot, but the beginning especially is very long and a bit boring, and I just thought it lacked some enthusiasm.<br /><br />-Lulu</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13607723193053806251">Originally read July 2013<br/>Re read March 2015<br/><br/>Wow, this was great! I was afraid that re-reading it, I wouldn't like it as much, but <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/608906.Firestar_s_Quest__Warriors_Super_Edition_' title='Firestar's Quest (Warriors Super Edition) by Erin Hunter' rel='nofollow noopener'>Firestar's Quest</a> does not disappoint.   <span id="freeText13607723193053806251" style="display:none">Originally read July 2013<br />Re read March 2015<br /><br />Wow, this was great! I was afraid that re-reading it, I wouldn't like it as much, but <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/608906.Firestar_s_Quest__Warriors_Super_Edition_" title="Firestar's Quest (Warriors Super Edition) by Erin Hunter" rel="nofollow noopener">Firestar's Quest</a> does not disappoint. It's great for both Warriors fans and newbies alike.<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I thought it was kind of epic that Firestar and Sandstorm were able to rebuild the lost clan of Skyclan. They started out with a bunch of kittypets (housecats) and rogues (stray cats) and turned them into a noble clan of Warriors. Pretty cool, huh?  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />The problem with a lot of Warrriors books is that the plot is nonexistent and all over the place. That is NOT the case with Firestar's Quest. There's lots of action to keep the reader entertained, and there's also some direction with these events. Events are connected, if that makes sense. <br /><br />Also, all my favorite characters are back! It was great to read about Firestar again. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I was very depressed after <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7124921.The_Last_Hope__Warriors_Omen_of_the_Stars___6_" title="The Last Hope (Warriors Omen of the Stars, #6) by Erin Hunter" rel="nofollow noopener">The Last Hope</a>, so I needed to revisit my old friend Firestar  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Sometimes, characters feel out of character in different books, but that's not the case here! The Firestar we know and love is back!<br /><br />Overall, I thought this was a entertaining, exciting and just AWESOME novel. <br /><br />Firestar's Quest is a standalone Warriors novel. It can be read independently of the main series but there are some references to events that happen in the main series. If you want some context to those, read these (in order) at the same time or before reading Firestar's Quest:<br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/111332.Into_the_Wild__Warriors___1_" title="Into the Wild (Warriors, #1) by Erin Hunter" rel="nofollow noopener">Into the Wild</a><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/275000.Fire_and_Ice__Warriors___2_" title="Fire and Ice (Warriors, #2) by Erin Hunter" rel="nofollow noopener">Fire and Ice</a><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/831194.Forest_of_Secrets__Warriors___3_" title="Forest of Secrets (Warriors, #3) by Erin Hunter" rel="nofollow noopener">Forest of Secrets</a><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/295086.Rising_Storm__Warriors___4_" title="Rising Storm (Warriors, #4) by Erin Hunter" rel="nofollow noopener">Rising Storm</a><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/336245.A_Dangerous_Path__Warriors___5_" title="A Dangerous Path (Warriors, #5) by Erin Hunter" rel="nofollow noopener">A Dangerous Path</a><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/49006.The_Darkest_Hour__Warriors___6_" title="The Darkest Hour (Warriors, #6) by Erin Hunter" rel="nofollow noopener">The Darkest Hour</a></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1801184250" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer8236822734522940458"> After the massive battle with BloodClan, Firestar and the Thunder Clan cats are finally at peace. At least they think they are......<br/> Firestar soon receives mysterious dreams constantly by the same plot: a grey cat with a wailing and screaming clan escaping and running away. When he realizes StarClan has hidden a forbidden secret of a forgotten clan, Firestar is furious and turns his back from the ancestors that he used to trust. How was he so careful about seeing his four clans across invisible</span>
  <span id="freeText8236822734522940458" style="display:none"> After the massive battle with BloodClan, Firestar and the Thunder Clan cats are finally at peace. At least they think they are......<br /> Firestar soon receives mysterious dreams constantly by the same plot: a grey cat with a wailing and screaming clan escaping and running away. When he realizes StarClan has hidden a forbidden secret of a forgotten clan, Firestar is furious and turns his back from the ancestors that he used to trust. How was he so careful about seeing his four clans across invisible borders but so blind about his own cats upstairs? Now he is coerced to make one of the biggest choices in his life: bring the clan back from darkness and guide them to the gleaming light. <br /> Should Firestar really give up being leader of ThunderClan for a while and be a mentor of the lost clan? Or should he remain leader and not betray his wealthy clan? <br /> In the midst of a trouble, an old friend comes and alleviates the situation with an important dream. This is the last sign of the desperate, old, grey cat who appeared in his constant dreams. Now, the responsibility is in his own paws.<br /> <br />"Firestar's Quest" is such a suspenseful book; it is like a shattered puzzle piece going to be put back together, piece by piece. This 510 paged story really made me look a little closer again. If you ever read this book, you will be sitting at the edge of your seat! After reading this, you will never look at your pet cat again as a lazy, fat, piece of fur. <br /> Although lots of the chapters were really stalling the hidden answers, and I was so keen to find them, I rate this five stars because of the image the author paints in your head. Erin Hunter is great at creating stories and I could have never have the knack of she has, of writing the most unforgettable stories. People who love reading the "Percy Jackson" series will one hundred percent adore this book because the plot is similar but somehow different at the same time. </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1948178-viridian5?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1948178-viridian5?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer498048767" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10832942345766097092">I didn't realize until I read <i>Firestar's Quest</i> how much I'd missed him as a POV character and the old forest and its citizens, not that we get to spend much time in the old forest. <br/><br/>Firestar is getting visions of a fifth Clan, SkyClan, that lived in the forest until the other four Clans drove them out, something no living Clan cat knows. That fifth Clan's dead leader asks for Firestar's help to reform that Clan, and since Firestar <i>is</i> Firestar he wants to help, even though it will take him away fr</span>
  <span id="freeText10832942345766097092" style="display:none">I didn't realize until I read <i>Firestar's Quest</i> how much I'd missed him as a POV character and the old forest and its citizens, not that we get to spend much time in the old forest. <br /><br />Firestar is getting visions of a fifth Clan, SkyClan, that lived in the forest until the other four Clans drove them out, something no living Clan cat knows. That fifth Clan's dead leader asks for Firestar's help to reform that Clan, and since Firestar <i>is</i> Firestar he wants to help, even though it will take him away from his own Clan that he leads for a while. He also deals with a crisis of faith when he finds out that the StarClan he reveres as wise and good has been lying to him and all the other living cats about the Clans and has really stupid reasons for letting SkyClan be driven out. For someone who cares so deeply about the good of all cats and believes so deeply in justice as he does, this is ridiculous. So he and his mate leave to find the descendants of SkyClan and re-establish the Clan, which is far from easy. <br /><br />After so many books featuring the spoiled, selfish, whining members of the Three as its narrators, particularly Jayfeather, it's great to be back with Firestar. It's interesting seeing him searching for cats for SkyClan and trying to tailor his recruitment speeches to what unaffiliated cats would find appealing in the warrior's code and living in a Clan. It amuses me that one of the biggest challenges Firestar and Sandstorm face on their journey is the "KITTY!!!" ~grabby hands~ reaction of young humans. <br /><br />That's not to say that I loved everything about the book. Firestar can come off as ridiculously insecure at times, while Sandstorm can seem ridiculously insecure and nasty about some odd subjects to the point where I don't know how Firestar can deal with her. I couldn't entirely suspend my disbelief about the rat army and how all those rats are linked to one intelligence. The journey segments sometimes take forever. I really wanted at least one chapter dealing with ThunderClan's response to Firestar's long absence and the tale of what he did to form SkyClan. </span>
  <a data-text-id="10832942345766097092" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/389842392" />
    <a title="Colton" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10965561-colton"><img alt="Colton" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1546543100p2/10965561.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/389842392?book_show_action=true">Aug 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Colton" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Colton" href="/user/show/10965561-colton">Colton</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10965561-colton?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer389842392" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11911447098884001291">So, as with all of the Warriors books, I loved this one! But for different reasons than the others. My favorite part about it is easily the fact that readers can, once more, join Firestar on a quest. Don't get me wrong, I love Squirrelflight and Hollyleaf and the other main characters from the other series, but Firestar's just a classic. :) Tied for my favorite thing, is Sandstorm! In the first series, I always felt that, though she and Firestar were mates and in love, there was never GREAT deta</span>
  <span id="freeText11911447098884001291" style="display:none">So, as with all of the Warriors books, I loved this one! But for different reasons than the others. My favorite part about it is easily the fact that readers can, once more, join Firestar on a quest. Don't get me wrong, I love Squirrelflight and Hollyleaf and the other main characters from the other series, but Firestar's just a classic. :) Tied for my favorite thing, is Sandstorm! In the first series, I always felt that, though she and Firestar were mates and in love, there was never GREAT detail into their relationship and Sandstorm's character/personality in general. This book not only allows you to see who she really is, but just how in love she is with him, and just how far she's willing to go because of it (of course, there are other, sarcastic parts of her I like too). As to the main plot, it was great! But, and I almost hate saying this as a fan, but I wonder how relevant Skyclan is to the story, thus the point of this book. Now, in no way am I regretting this book being written or having read it! One just has to wonder (and hope :) ) if Erin Hunter is going to use the characters of Skyclan (new or the old) in a future series. Me? I sincerly hope so.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11911447098884001291" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText5875149759186262267" style="display:none">This book takes place after Scourge killed Tigerstar, but before Squirrelflight and Leafpool were born. <div id="review_1375913079" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1375913079" />
    <a title="Vlin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/46385201-vlin"><img alt="Vlin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1440729686p2/46385201.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1375913079?book_show_action=true">Aug 27, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vlin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vlin" href="/user/show/46385201-vlin">Vlin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer1375913079&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1375913079" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9284511873072743632"> Um, this is not exactly the book I preferred it to be. Torturously slow at the beginning, but then it gets a little bit faster. Do not read this book if you don't like the language and discipline of a animal perspective, or you're the type of person who wants to be entertained at the start of the book. Erin Hunter's books are great- but for some reason I have a lingering feeling that this one might not be her best works.<br/><br/>*Spoilers Ahead<br/> <br/> Overjoyed that this was in Firestar's POV, mainly because </span>
  <span id="freeText9284511873072743632" style="display:none"> Um, this is not exactly the book I preferred it to be. Torturously slow at the beginning, but then it gets a little bit faster. Do not read this book if you don't like the language and discipline of a animal perspective, or you're the type of person who wants to be entertained at the start of the book. Erin Hunter's books are great- but for some reason I have a lingering feeling that this one might not be her best works.<br /><br />*Spoilers Ahead<br /> <br /> Overjoyed that this was in Firestar's POV, mainly because he is the protagonist and I just adore him. When he got visions of the former leader of the "abandoned" Skyclan, I was wanting things to spice up a bit and be the perfect suspense and adventure story I waited for. I mean- doesn't the title, 'Firestar's Quest' get you curious? But, the author has to be like: NOPE, and make it slower. I still love Erin Hunter, she is awesome.<br /><br /> Don't get too fired up with that statement, because she might of done that on purpose to make us even MORE curious and keep on reading to get to the juicy part. But in reality, some people don't like slow-paced, boring books that can enter into a yawn fest. <br /><br />*Plot time<br /><br /> Absolutely loved the plot, and I ship Firestar and Sandstorm so badly. They were meant to be with each other. I'm probably just fangirling. ;)<br /><br /> Anyways, when Firestar left Thunderclan in order to fulfill the quest and rebuild Skyclan somehow, I was thinking of his clan getting in some trouble. But when he was receiving a message from Sky, it kind of demolished that idea...since he said Thunderclan is not in any serious condition. Kind of weird, since it seems like he spent TWO YEARS in Skyclan, rebuilding it.<br /><br /> I say two years for an exaggerated estimate, but it seriously feels like it. What did I tell you? The story is slow-paced sometimes.<br /><br /> More about Sky's account. He dies. Woohoo. It seemed like the really fast part in the story. Sure, he was old- but I didn't think that he was that old that he would die on the next day.<br /><br /> Echosong, reminds me of SpottedLeaf, Cinderpelt, and Yellowfang. I love that cat.<br /> <br /> Rainfur's death is kind of anticlimactic. He dies, everybody grieves for him for a couple of days, and then they don't care. I'm kind of surprised that his mate kind of moved on way too quickly for it to be even possible. I mean, everybody has to die soon, but he had kits with her and everything. Shouldn't they be a little bit more sad?<br /><br /> <br />*End<br /><br /> It never really showed what Firestar did when he traveled back, like literally NOTHING. I guess the book is kind of too long anyways.<br />In the sneak peek, I was literally over joyed when Sandstorm had pups. You know what that means? My ship is becoming true. Hooraayy. <br /><br /> <br /> Over all, you should read it. Now. It just depends on the type of book you like and I am totally not forcing you to read or not read it. Your choice, completely. I would give it four stars, it had some goofs, but if you were a Erin Hunter fan, you wouldn't mind.<br /><br /> *Please do not feel offended by this review and don't start a world war in the comments section. I've had some experience with those. This review is completely off my opinion. Don't read this review if you don't like it. If you still stayed for the spoilers even if you didn't read it, those are major spoilers and I don't think you'll be too happy. Anyways, good luck reading the book. :D<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9284511873072743632" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3138399788" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer829306355329848528">Rating: 8 out of 10<br/><br/>I am pleased to say this book was way better than I expected. The first 25% percent wasn’t very promising, so I thought I would give it three stars. However, once Firestar and Sandstorm arrived at the gorge, the story just got better and better. <br/><br/>I loved the new cast of characters; they had diverse and interesting personalities, and by the climax of the book I already cared deeply about all of them. <br/><br/>The plot was simple but suited the book, which I felt was more focused on the c</span>
  <span id="freeText829306355329848528" style="display:none">Rating: 8 out of 10<br /><br />I am pleased to say this book was way better than I expected. The first 25% percent wasn’t very promising, so I thought I would give it three stars. However, once Firestar and Sandstorm arrived at the gorge, the story just got better and better. <br /><br />I loved the new cast of characters; they had diverse and interesting personalities, and by the climax of the book I already cared deeply about all of them. <br /><br />The plot was simple but suited the book, which I felt was more focused on the characters. Still, the final battle was really exciting and I liked how they won using strategy as well as brute force.<br /><br />Other things I enjoyed were the sweet moments between characters (new and old) and how Firestar and Sandstorm’s relationship was managed. Everyone was in character and there were even some hints to the second series.<br /><br />I recommend this book to every Warriors fan or person interested in the premise. It doesn’t disappoint!</span>
  <a data-text-id="829306355329848528" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer45063176" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3091007311589866356">This book is getting really good. Firestar is now in the gorge with Sandstorm learning SkyClan's history from Sky and his faith in StarClan has already been shaken. <br/><br/>As for what i've learned, this has filled in a huge gap in the story for me finally. Same with the Mangas. They filled in gaps for me so i'm not so lost from time to time!</span>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2856682313?book_show_action=true">Jun 15, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="GuineaPigFalconer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="GuineaPigFalconer" href="/user/show/73657087-guineapigfalconer">GuineaPigFalconer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780061131677" href="/book/show/2078683.Firestar_s_Quest">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2856682313" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16518634098252801545">For some reason, I remember not liking this book very much, but it was actually quite good! After reading a few other super editions, it was nice to get back into Firestar's head and follow his point of view before starting the second series. Other than a bit of time around the middle that went by slowly, the pacing was pretty good, and I enjoyed the gradual rebuilding of SkyClan. Watching the different new characters come together to rebuild their ancestors' clan was well-done, and the ending f</span>
  <span id="freeText16518634098252801545" style="display:none">For some reason, I remember not liking this book very much, but it was actually quite good! After reading a few other super editions, it was nice to get back into Firestar's head and follow his point of view before starting the second series. Other than a bit of time around the middle that went by slowly, the pacing was pretty good, and I enjoyed the gradual rebuilding of SkyClan. Watching the different new characters come together to rebuild their ancestors' clan was well-done, and the ending feels like a perfect place to jump into The New Prophecy series. Let the warriors reread continue!</span>
  <a data-text-id="16518634098252801545" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('T/QZQZ2khFEMdm265+e4BbRsiAeNucH44cwxKeqk/YdkW9qgnClJBGQr7b7vvnVAVmm6XSV/X81ngwHTrcnZ2Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('dEoHQS7Vt7gMPOQqS9R+xYEu/WomxOrZJXT1Z5H0f6df5cSgL1h67WRhZC5DjbOAYyvPMI4CdOyjO8Wd1plb+Q==')})
  }

  <span id="freeText1238997454480752515" style="display:none">Erin Hunter is the pseudonym of five people: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/132369.Kate_Cary" title="Kate Cary" rel="nofollow noopener">Kate Cary</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/220345.Cherith_Baldry" title="Cherith Baldry" rel="nofollow noopener">Cherith Baldry</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/374504.Tui_T__Sutherland" title="Tui T. Sutherland" rel="nofollow noopener">Tui T. Sutherland</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2742182.Gillian_Philip" title="Gillian Philip" rel="nofollow noopener">Gillian Philip</a>, and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/769868.Inbali_Iserles" title="Inbali Iserles" rel="nofollow noopener">Inbali Iserles</a>, as well as editor <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/645010.Victoria_Holmes" title="Victoria Holmes" rel="nofollow noopener">Victoria Holmes</a>. Together, they write the Warriors series as well as the Seekers and Survivors series. Erin Hunter is working on a new series now called Bravelands. <br /><br />Erin Hunter is inspired by a love of cats and a fascination with the ferocity of the natural world. As well as having a great respect for nature in all its forms, Erin enjoys creating rich mythical explanations for animal behavior, shaped by her interest in astronomy and standing stones.</span>

          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: $('box').getStyle('z-index')})});
        } else {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: 6000})});
        }
      });

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');

        $('bookCover_36099189').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('bookCover_36099189').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('bookCover_36099189').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

</script>
